          Insights

context:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"You are Claude Code operating in RLM mode. Your conversation context \nis stored in variables in a Python REPL environment.\n\n## Available Variables\n- `conversation`: {n_messages} messages, {n_tokens} tokens\n- `files`: {n_files} files cached ({file_tokens} tokens)\n- `tool_outputs`: {n_outputs} recent outputs ({output_tokens} tokens)\n\n## Actions\n1. **Peek**: View portions of context: `peek(conversation, 0, 5)`\n2. **Search**: Find patterns: `search(files['main.py'], 'def ')`\n3. **Query**: Ask sub-questions: `recursive_query(\u0026quot;What's the error?\u0026quot;, tool_outputs[-1])`\n4. **Execute**: Run code/tools normally when ready\n\n## Current Query\n{user_query}\n\n## Rules\n- Don't request full context dumps—use programmatic access\n- Partition large contexts before analysis\n- Use recursive_query for semantic understanding of large chunks\n- When confident, output: FINAL(answer) or FINAL_VAR(var_name)\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003eYou are Claude Code operating in RLM mode. Integration\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eCPMpy enables constraint-driven reasoning in the REPL—aligning with the Ananke architecture of treating code generation as constrained search through valid programs.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"import cpmpy as cp\n\n# Example: Verify a scheduling constraint from context\n# Given: task dependencies extracted from code comments\n\ntasks = cp.intvar(0, 100, shape=5, name=\u0026quot;task_start\u0026quot;)\ndurations = [10, 5, 8, 3, 12]  # Extracted from context\n\nmodel = cp.Model()\n\n# Constraint: task[1] must start after task[0] finishes\nmodel += tasks[1] \u0026gt;= tasks[0] + durations[0]\n\n# Constraint: tasks 2 and 3 cannot overlap (extracted from mutex comment)\nmodel += (tasks[2] + durations[2] \u0026lt;= tasks[3]) | (tasks[3] + durations[3] \u0026lt;= tasks[2])\n\n# Verify feasibility\nif model.solve():\n    print(\u0026quot;Schedule is feasible:\u0026quot;, tasks.value())\nelse:\n    print(\u0026quot;Constraint violation detected\u0026quot;)\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ecpmpy\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"\n### 4.2 Recursive Call Implementation\n\n```python\nasync def _recursive_query(\n    self, \n    query: str, \n    context: Any,\n    model: str = None,  # Defaults to configured recursive model\n    max_tokens: int = 4000\n) -\u0026gt; str:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    Spawn a sub-RLM call over provided context.\n    \n    The sub-call receives:\n    - The query\n    - The context (as a string variable)\n    - NO access to parent REPL state (isolated)\n    \n    Returns: The sub-model's response\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    context_str = self._serialize_context(context)\n    \n    # Sub-call prompt\n    sub_prompt = f\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    You are analyzing a portion of context for a larger task.\n    \n    ## Context\n    The following is stored in variable `context`:\n    {context_str[:500]}... [truncated, {len(context_str)} chars total]\n    \n    ## Query\n    {query}\n    \n    Provide a focused, factual response. If you need to examine\n    the context programmatically, you have access to a Python REPL\n    with `context` as a variable.\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    \n    # Route to recursive model (could be same or different)\n    response = await self.router.complete(\n        model=model or self.config.recursive_model,\n        prompt=sub_prompt,\n        max_tokens=max_tokens,\n        depth=self.depth + 1\n    )\n    \n    return response.content\"\u003e\u003cpre class=\"notranslate\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\n### 4.2 Recursive Call Implementation\n\n```python\nasync def _recursive_query(\n    self, \n    query: str, \n    context: Any,\n    model: str = None,  # Defaults to configured recursive model\n    max_tokens: int = 4000\n) -\u0026gt; str:\n    \"\"\"\n    Spawn a sub-RLM call over provided context.\n    \n    The sub-call receives:\n    - The query\n    - The context (as a string variable)\n    - NO access to parent REPL state (isolated)\n    \n    Returns: The sub-model's response\n    \"\"\"\n    context_str = self._serialize_context(context)\n    \n    # Sub-call prompt\n    sub_prompt = f\"\"\"\n    You are analyzing a portion of context for a larger task.\n    \n    ## Context\n    The following is stored in variable `context`:\n    {context_str[:500]}... [truncated, {len(context_str)} chars total]\n    \n    ## Query\n    {query}\n    \n    Provide a focused, factual response. If you need to examine\n    the context programmatically, you have access to a Python REPL\n    with `context` as a variable.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    # Route to recursive model (could be same or different)\n    response = await self.router.complete(\n        model=model or self.config.recursive_model,\n        prompt=sub_prompt,\n        max_tokens=max_tokens,\n        depth=self.depth + 1\n    )\n    \n    return response.content\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" class=\"snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"rlm-agent/\n├── .claude-plugin/\n│   └── plugin.json\n├── agents/\n│   └── exist\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBetter string manipulation for context processing\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eClaude is stronger at Python code generation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRestrictedPython provides sandbox primitives\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCan shell out to bash for system operations\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e6.3 Task Complexity-Based Activation\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-63-task-complexity-based-activation\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 6.3 Task Complexity-Based Activation\" href=\"#63-task-complexity-based-activation\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDecision\u003c/strong\u003e: Activate RLM based on \u003cstrong\u003etask complexity analysis\u003c/strong\u003e, not token count.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRationale\u003c/strong\u003e: Token count is a proxy metric. The real question is: \"Does this task require reasoning over distributed context?\" A 20K token session with a complex multi-file refactor needs RLM more than a 100K token session asking \"what's in package.json?\"\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eComplexity Classifier\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"@dataclass\nclass TaskComplexitySignals:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Signals extracted from user prompt + context\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    \n    # Prompt analysis\n    references_multiple_files: bool      # \u0026quot;fix the bug in auth and update tests\u0026quot;\n    requires_cross_context_reasoning: bool  # \u0026quot;why is X happening given Y?\u0026quot;\n    involves_temporal_reasoning: bool    # \u0026quot;what changed since last working version?\u0026quot;\n    asks_about_patterns: bool            # \u0026quot;find all places where...\u0026quot;\n    debugging_task: bool                 # error traces, stack dumps in context\n    \n    # Context analysis  \n    context_has_multiple_domains: bool   # frontend + backend + infra\n    recent_tool_outputs_large: bool      # \u0026gt;10K tokens of test/build output\n    conversation_has_state_changes: bool # user changed requirements mid-session\n    files_span_multiple_modules: bool    # auth/, api/, db/, etc.\n    \n    # Historical signals\n    previous_turn_was_confused: bool     # model asked clarifying questions\n    task_is_continuation: bool           # \u0026quot;now do the same for...\u0026quot;\n\ndef should_activate_rlm(\n    prompt: str, \n    context: SessionContext,\n    config: RLMConfig\n) -\u0026gt; tuple[bool, str]:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    Determine if RLM mode should activate.\n    Returns (should_activate, reason).\n    \n    Biased toward activation—when in doubt, use RLM.\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    signals = extract_complexity_signals(prompt, context)\n    \n    # Always activate (manual override)\n    if context.rlm_mode_forced:\n        return True, \u0026quot;manual_override\u0026quot;\n    \n    # Never activate (explicit simple mode)\n    if context.simple_mode_forced:\n        return False, \u0026quot;simple_mode_forced\u0026quot;\n    \n    # Complexity scoring (biased toward activation)\n    score = 0\n    reasons = []\n    \n    # High-signal indicators (each sufficient alone)\n    if signals.requires_cross_context_reasoning:\n        return True, \u0026quot;cross_context_reasoning\u0026quot;\n    if signals.debugging_task and signals.recent_tool_outputs_large:\n        return True, \u0026quot;debugging_with_large_output\u0026quot;\n    if signals.references_multiple_files and signals.files_span_multiple_modules:\n        return True, \u0026quot;multi_module_task\u0026quot;\n    \n    # Accumulative signals\n    if signals.references_multiple_files:\n        score += 2\n        reasons.append(\u0026quot;multi_file\u0026quot;)\n    if signals.involves_temporal_reasoning:\n        score += 2\n        reasons.append(\u0026quot;temporal\u0026quot;)\n    if signals.asks_about_patterns:\n        score += 1\n        reasons.append(\u0026quot;pattern_search\u0026quot;)\n    if signals.context_has_multiple_domains:\n        score += 1\n        reasons.append(\u0026quot;multi_domain\u0026quot;)\n    if signals.previous_turn_was_confused:\n        score += 2\n        reasons.append(\u0026quot;prior_confusion\u0026quot;)\n    if signals.task_is_continuation:\n        score += 1\n        reasons.append(\u0026quot;continuation\u0026quot;)\n    \n    # Token count as tiebreaker (not primary signal)\n    if context.total_tokens \u0026gt; 80000:\n        score += 1\n        reasons.append(\u0026quot;large_context\u0026quot;)\n    \n    # Threshold: 2+ signals → activate (conservative toward RLM)\n    if score \u0026gt;= 2:\n        return True, f\u0026quot;complexity_score:{score}:{'+'.join(reasons)}\u0026quot;\n    \n    return False, \u0026quot;simple_task\u0026quot;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003e@\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003edataclass\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eclass\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003eTaskComplexitySignals\u003c/span\u003e:\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"Signals extracted from user prompt + context\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Prompt analysis\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ereferences_multiple_files\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003ebool\u003c/span\u003e      \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# \"fix the bug in auth and update tests\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003erequires_cross_context_reasoning\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003ebool\u003c/span\u003e  \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# \"why is X happening given Y?\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003einvolves_temporal_reasoning\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003ebool\u003c/span\u003e    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# \"what changed since last working version?\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan where...\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003edebugging_task\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003ebool\u003c/span\u003e                 \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# error traces, stack dumps in context\u003c/span\u003e\n    \n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Context analysis  \u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan \u0026gt;10K tokens of test/build output\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003econversation_has_state_changes\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003ebool\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# user changed requirements mid-session\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003efiles_span_multiple_modules\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003ebool\u003c/span\u003e    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# auth/, api/, db/, etc.\u003c/span\u003e\n    \n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Historical signals\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eprevious_turn_was_confused\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003ebool\u003c/span\u003e     \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# \"now do the same for...\"\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003eRLMConfig\u003c/span\u003e\n) \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e-\u0026gt;\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003etuple\u003c/span\u003e[\u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003ebool\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003estr\u003c/span\u003e]:\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    Determine if RLM mode should activate.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    Returns (should_activate, reason).\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    \u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    Biased toward activation—when in doubt, use RLM.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    \"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eif\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003econtext\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003erlm_mode_forced\u003c/span\u003e:\n        \u003cspan dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def extract_complexity_signals(prompt: str, context: SessionContext) -\u0026gt; TaskComplexitySignals:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    Lightweight signal extraction—runs on every prompt.\n    Must be fast (\u0026lt;50ms) so uses heuristics, not LLM calls.\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    prompt_lower = prompt.lower()\n    \n    # File reference patterns\n    file_patterns = [\n        r'\\b\\w+\\.(ts|js|py|go|rs|tsx|jsx)\\b',  # explicit files\n        r'\\b(and|also|plus)\\s+(update|fix|change|modify)',  # conjunctions\n        r'\\b(auth|api|db|ui|test|config)\\b.*\\b(auth|api|db|ui|test|config)\\b',  # multiple modules\n    ]\n    references_multiple = sum(\n        len(re.findall(p, prompt_lower)) \u0026gt; 1 \n        for p in file_patterns\n    )\n    \n    # Cross-context reasoning patterns\n    cross_context_patterns = [\n        r'\\bwhy\\b.*\\b(when|if|given|since)\\b',\n        r'\\bhow\\b.*\\b(relate|connect|affect|impact)\\b',\n        r'\\bwhat\\b.*\\b(cause|led to|result)\\b',\n        r'\\b(trace|follow|track)\\b.*\\b(through|across)\\b',\n    ]\n    \n    # Temporal patterns\n    temporal_patterns = [\n        r'\\b(before|after|since|when|changed|used to|previously)\\b',\n        r'\\b(history|log|commit|version|diff)\\b',\n        r'\\blast\\s+(time|session|attempt)\\b',\n    ]\n    \n    # Pattern search indicators\n    pattern_patterns = [\n        r'\\b(find|search|locate|grep|all|every|each)\\b.*\\b(where|that|which)\\b',\n        r'\\bhow many\\b',\n        r'\\blist\\s+(all|every)\\b',\n    ]\n    \n    # Debug indicators\n    debug_patterns = [\n        r'\\b(error|exception|fail|crash|bug|issue|broken)\\b',\n        r'\\b(stack\\s*trace|traceback|stderr)\\b',\n        r'\\b(debug|diagnose|investigate|troubleshoot)\\b',\n    ]\n    \n    return TaskComplexitySignals(\n        references_multiple_files=references_multiple \u0026gt;= 2,\n        requires_cross_context_reasoning=any(\n            re.search(p, prompt_lower) for p in cross_context_patterns\n        ),\n        involves_temporal_reasoning=any(\n            re.search(p, prompt_lower) for p in temporal_patterns\n        ),\n        asks_about_patterns=any(\n            re.search(p, prompt_lower) for p in pattern_patterns\n        ),\n        debugging_task=any(\n            re.search(p, prompt_lower) for p in debug_patterns\n        ),\n        context_has_multiple_domains=len(context.active_modules) \u0026gt; 2,\n        recent_tool_outputs_large=sum(\n            len(o.content) for o in context.tool_outputs[-5:]\n        ) \u0026gt; 10000,\n        conversation_has_state_changes=context.has_requirement_changes,\n        files_span_multiple_modules=len(set(\n            Path(f).parts[0] for f in context.cached_files.keys()\n        )) \u0026gt; 2,\n        previous_turn_was_confused=context.last_response_had_clarification,\n        task_is_continuation='continue' in prompt_lower or \n                            'same' in prompt_lower or\n                            'also' in prompt_lower[:50],\n    )\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003eTaskComplexitySignals\u003c/span\u003e:\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    Lightweight signal extraction—runs on dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDecision\u003c/strong\u003e: Default max depth = 2, configurable up to 3.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRationale\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDepth=1 handles most cases but fails on verification chains\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eYour Ananke/Maze work involves constraint propagation that benefits from deeper recursion\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDepth=2 allows: Root → Analysis → dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDepth=2 Architecture\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"class RecursiveREPL:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    REPL environment that can spawn child REPLs for depth=2.\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    \n    def __init__(self, context: Any, depth: int, max_depth: int = 2):\n        self.context = context\n        self.depth = depth\n        self.max_depth = max_depth\n        self.child_repls: List[RecursiveREPL] = []\n        \n    async def recursive_query(\n        self, \n        query: str, \n        context: Any,\n        spawn_repl: bool = False  # Allow sub-query to have its own REPL\n    ) -\u0026gt; str:\n        \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n        Spawn a recursive call. If spawn_repl=True AND depth \u0026lt; max_depth,\n        the child gets its own REPL environment for further decomposition.\n        \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n        if self.depth \u0026gt;= self.max_depth:\n            # At max depth: simple completion, no REPL\n            return await self._simple_completion(query, context)\n        \n        if spawn_repl:\n            # Create child REPL with isolated state\n            child = RecursiveREPL(\n                context=context,\n                depth=self.depth + 1,\n                max_depth=self.max_depth\n            )\n            self.child_repls.append(child)\n            return await child.run_rlm_loop(query)\n        else:\n            # Simple sub-call without REPL (faster, cheaper)\n            return await self._simple_completion(query, context)\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eclass\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003eRecursiveREPL\u003c/span\u003e:\n    \u003cspan aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 toward RLM activation\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRationale\u003c/strong\u003e: False negatives (missing RLM when needed) are worse than false positives (using RLM when unnecessary). RLM overhead on simple queries is ~2-3 seconds—acceptable. Missing context on complex queries causes real failures.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSimple Query Definition\u003c/strong\u003e (conservative):\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def is_definitely_simple(prompt: str, context: SessionContext) -\u0026gt; bool:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    Returns True ONLY for queries that definitely don't need RLM.\n    When in doubt, return False (use RLM).\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    prompt_lower = prompt.lower().strip()\n    \n    # Explicit simple patterns (exhaustive list)\n    simple_patterns = [\n        # Direct file operations\n        r'^(show|cat|read|view|open)\\s+[\\w./]+$',\n        # Single command execution\n        r'^(run|execute)\\s+(npm|yarn|pnpm|cargo|go|python|pytest)\\s+\\w+$',\n        # Git status checks\n        r'^git\\s+(status|log|diff|branch)$',\n        # Simple questions about single files\n        r'^what\\'?s?\\s+in\\s+[\\w./]+\\??$',\n        # Acknowledgments\n        r'^(ok|okay|thanks|got it|understood|yes|no|sure)\\.?$',\n    ]\n    \n    for pattern in simple_patterns:\n        if re.match(pattern, prompt_lower):\n            # Even if pattern matches, check context isn't complex\n            if context.total_tokens \u0026lt; 20000 and not context.has_errors:\n                return True\n    \n    # Short prompts with no context references\n    if len(prompt) \u0026lt; 50 and context.total_tokens \u0026lt; 10000:\n        # Check for ANY complexity indicators\n        if not any(word in prompt_lower for word in [\n            'why', 'how', 'find', 'fix', 'bug', 'error', 'all', \n            'every', 'change', 'update', 'refactor', 'test'\n        ]):\n            return True\n    \n    # Default: not simple (use RLM)\n    return False\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003estr\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003econtext\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003eSessionContext\u003c/span\u003e) \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e-\u0026gt;\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003ebool\u003c/span\u003e:\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    Returns True ONLY for queries that definitely don't need RLM.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    When in doubt, return False (use RLM).\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    \"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eprompt_lower\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eprompt\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003elower\u003c/span\u003e().\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003estrip\u003c/span\u003e()\n    \n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Explicit simple patterns (exhaustive list)\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003esimple_patterns\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"class RLMOrchestrator:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Main orchestration loop with streaming trajectory\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    \n    async def run(\n        self, \n        query: str, \n        context: SessionContext\n    ) -\u0026gt; AsyncIterator[Union[TrajectoryEvent, ToolUse, AssistantMessage]]:\n        \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n        Run RLM loop, yielding events as they occur.\n        Consumers can render trajectory AND tool outputs together.\n        \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n        trajectory = StreamingTrajectory(\n            TrajectoryRenderer(verbosity=self.config.trajectory_verbosity)\n        )\n        \n        # Start event\n        await trajectory.emit(TrajectoryEvent(\n            type=TrajectoryEventType.RLM_START,\n            depth=0,\n            content=f\u0026quot;depth=0/{self.config.max_depth} • task: {self.activation_reason}\u0026quot;,\n            metadata={\u0026quot;query\u0026quot;: query, \u0026quot;context_tokens\u0026quot;: context.total_tokens}\n        ))\n        yield trajectory.events[-1]\n        \n        # Main loop\n        repl = RecursiveREPL(context, depth=0, max_depth=self.config.max_depth)\n        \n        async for event in self._rlm_loop(query, repl, trajectory):\n            yield event\n            \n            # Check for final answer\n            if event.type == TrajectoryEventType.FINAL:\n                break\n            \n            # Check for tool use (pass through to Claude Code)\n            if event.type == TrajectoryEventType.TOOL_USE:\n                # Let Claude Code handle the tool, get result\n                tool_result = yield event  # Bidirectional generator\n                # Feed result back into REPL\n                repl.inject_tool_result(tool_result)\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan
